replication protocol is implemented across multiple Java and Scala source files. The core components are:\\n\\n1. **ReplicaFetcherThread** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala) - The main thread responsible for a follower/replica fetching data from the leader. It extends AbstractFetcherThread and implements processPartitionData() which handles incoming data from the leader, updates log offsets, and manages high watermark updates.\\n\\n2. **LeaderEpochFileCache** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java) - A critical component that maintains a cache of (LeaderEpoch => Offset) mappings for each replica. This enables the replica to determine where to truncate its log during leader elections or when recovering from divergence. The cache is persisted asynchronously through a checkpoint file.\\n\\n3. **LogStartOffset Tracking** (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java) - The UnifiedLog class maintains both logStartOffset and localLogStartOffset fields. LogStartOffset tracks the earliest readable message offset globally, while localLogStartOffset tracks the local start after log retention policies. ReplicaFetcherThread updates these via maybeIncrementLogStartOffset().\\n\\n4. **ISR Management** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala) - The Partition class implements two critical methods:\\n   - maybeExpandIsr(): Adds a follower replica back to the in-sync replicas set when it catches up with the leader\\n   - maybeShrinkIsr(): Removes a replica from the ISR when it falls too far behind (replica.lag.time.max.ms threshold)\\n   - Both methods interact with AlterPartitionManager to persist ISR changes to the controller\\n\\n5. **AbstractFetcherThread** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherThread.scala) - The abstract base class for all fetcher threads, implementing the core fetch loop. Key methods include doWork() which orchestrates the fetching process, and getOffsetTruncationState() which calculates truncation offsets based on leader epoch information.\\n\\n6. **ReplicaManager** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala) - Orchestrates replica management, owns the ReplicaFetcherManager and AlterPartitionManager, tracks ISR change metrics (isrExpandRate, isrShrinkRate), and manages the maybeShrinkIsr() periodic task.\\n\\n7. **ReplicaFetcherManager** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherManager.scala) - Manages pools of ReplicaFetcherThread instances, creating and routing partitions to appropriate fetcher threads based on leader assignment.\\n\\n8. **RemoteLeaderEndPoint** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/RemoteLeaderEndPoint.scala) - Represents a remote broker as a leader endpoint. Handles protocol communication including fetchOffset(), endOffsetForEpoch(), and manages fetch session state.\\n\\n9. **LocalLeaderEndPoint** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/LocalLeaderEndPoint.scala) - Represents the local broker as a leader endpoint, providing direct in-process access to leader state without network calls.\\n\\n10. **AlterPartitionManager** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AlterPartitionManager.scala) - Manages ISR updates by batching and sending AlterPartition requests to the controller. Maintains unsentIsrUpdates and inflightRequest state for proper ordering and idempotency.\\n\\n11. **AbstractFetcherManager** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherManager.scala) - Generic base class managing pools of fetcher threads, handling partition assignment and load balancing across threads.\\n\\n12. **TierStateMachine** (core/src/main/java/kafka/server/TierStateMachine.java) - Manages state transitions for tiered storage, handling cases where data has been moved to remote tier and determining correct fetch offsets.\\n\\n13. **ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread.scala) - Similar to ReplicaFetcherThread but for moving replicas between log directories, using the same epoch-based truncation mechanism.\\n\\nThe protocol flow: When a follower needs to replicate, ReplicaFetcherManager creates a ReplicaFetcherThread connected to the leader. The thread continuously fetches batches of records, appends them via Partition.appendRecordsToFollowerOrFutureReplica(), updates LogStartOffset based on leader feedback, manages truncation via endOffsetForEpoch() calls that return epoch boundaries, and participates in ISR updates when replication lag changes. The LeaderEpochFileCache enables safe recovery by tracking which offsets correspond to which leader epochs, preventing data loss during leader changes.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":13341,"cache_read_input_tokens":86918,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":13341},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"17371aed-4767-4797-94fa-00af9436a1a7","uuid":"5b006bf1-43a0-4b56-beeb-e67cbe244248"}
